BOOKS FROM NOTRE DAME 
The Bible and 1ha Liturgy 
Jean Danielou, S. J. 
The S_acramental rites of the Church-Baptism, Con­firmation, Holy Eucharist and great feasts of the liturgi­cal year-were designed to be an unfailing source of grace and meaning in the Christian life. Now, due to lack of mstruction, the rites are too often seen as curi­osities with no message for today's Christians. To remedy this situation Father Danielou examines the sign language of the Sacraments via modern scholar­ship in easily understandable language. This study will prove invaluable to those interested in learning and teaching the meaning of Christianity. October. $5.25 
Christian Democracy in Western Europe, 
1814-1952 
M. P. Fogarty 
A comprehensive study of the Christian Democratic movements in England, France, Italy, Germany, Bel­gium and the Netherlands. The author has not limited himself to a political history, but has compiled a far­ranging account of the richness of Christian Democratic social thought. December. $6.75 
The fate of East Central Europe: Hopes and Failures of American Foreign Policy Edited by Stephen D. Kertesz 
How the nations of East Central Europe came under Communist domination and what part American policy played in this vital area is the subject of th.is book. President Emeritus Charles Seymour of Yale says, "This book faces courageously and objectively the critical issue of United States policy toward East Central Europe. It provides the historical background essential to an understanding of the issue ... The distinction of the authors of the various chapters assures the validity of their approach to this vital problem." 
October. $6.25 

The Ancrene Riwle 
Edited and translated by M. B. Saha 
The complete text in modern English of this classic of mediaeval spirituality, with critical notes and references. The book contains a preface by Professor J. R. R. Tolkien and an introduction and appendix by Dom Gerard Sitwell. October. $2.75 



RECENTLY PUBLISHED 
The Mystery of the Woman 
Edited by Edward D. O'Connor, C.S.C. 
A simple and profound explanation of the three Marian dogmas which have made the greatest impact on the life of the Church, written by three outstanding Ameri­can Theologians, Walter Burghardt, S.J., Ferrer Smith, O.P., and Monsignor George Shea. $2.75 
Church Building and Furnishing 
J. B. O'Connell 
An indispensable tool for pastor and architect-the onlyone-volume book that brings together all the official regulations governing the building, furnishing and decorating of Catholic Churches. This compact refer­ance work contains, in an orderly and readily accessible form, the canons, rubrics and prescriptions concerningchurch architecture. The book's many beautiful illus­trations will prove of great value by demonstrating how wide is the range of technical solutions open to those who wish to build in accordance with the mind of the Church. 44 ruustrations. $5.50 
Liturgical Piety 
Pere Louis Bouyer 
Our Land and Our lady Daniel Sargent 
Traces the hand of Our Lady through the early history of America. Mr. Sargent interprets early ,beginnings and the later history of Catholicism in this country in terms of Our Blessed Mother. The struggle for Catholic edu­cation is well brought out. This story of missionary beginnings, strivings, failures and ultimate success is told with profound spirituality. $3.50 
Men in the Field 
Leo J. Ward, C.S.C. 
18 powerful short stories of Midwestern farm life of a generation ago. A cross section of life is laid bare-the people in all their pitiful and wonderful human variety are viewed with compassion and respect, portrayed with tenderness and strength. Father Ward's realistic stories hold more than the exact detail of corn farm life, they hold its spirit. $3.50
